Current Affairs Commentary

Shenxin No. 7 Factory Auction Incident

— Yan

At a time when Shanghai's economy is in depression and various industries and financial circles are running around to rescue the market, unexpectedly, HSBC Bank, as the first pledgee, entrusted Rouice Moyer & Co. to announce the auction of the factory base, houses, and machinery of Shenxin Yarn Factory No. 7. The industry, with a value of more than 5 million yuan, had a limited price of only 2.25 million yuan. Although the Bank of China and the Bank of Shanghai, also as creditors, applied to the First Special District Court for provisional attachment, and the court ruled to implement it, and business groups such as the Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the central government to find a way to stop it in order to protect property rights and industry, under special forces, Mr. Murakami, a Japanese lawyer representing a certain party, purchased it at the lowest bid price yesterday. We believe that HSBC Bank's move, if it were in a boom period, would not be criticized, but it is being published today when credit is extremely tight, so it must be regarded as a great regret and considered to have serious significance.

Tracing back to the tension in the Far East situation, the British have different views, and their policies towards China have not been consistent. The front line in China is quite fragmented. One faction, represented by HSBC Bank, adopted a strategy of abandoning the rights and interests of North China and the Yangtze River Basin, and transferring cash stored in Shanghai to Hong Kong to preserve its strength and wait for political developments. However, due to excessive cash transportation, the inventory was slightly empty, and a run on deposits once occurred last year. Although it calmed down soon, it might not have been so quick without the help of Chinese banks. Later, the bank authorities made preparations for Chinese deposits and had a plan to absorb cash. The long-discontinued banknotes were re-promoted and used indirectly by various foreign firms. Expiring deposits were attracted with high interest rates to prevent them from flowing out. All of these are factual manifestations of the bank's strategy.

Therefore, we believe that HSBC Bank's auction of Shenxin No. 7 Factory is actually a necessary stage to implement its recent China policy. The purpose is not only the one household of Shenxin No. 7 Factory. Unfortunately, "Shen No. 7" was sacrificed under the first trial of their bull knife. Speaking from HSBC Bank's standpoint, if this kind of extraordinary means is not adopted, the debts in Shanghai cannot be quickly settled. It seems that there are reasons for doing this urgently. However, the attitude of disregarding property rights and disregarding it decisively makes people turn pale at the mention of a tiger. Strengthening Sino-British friendship to benefit commerce should be what the general British businessmen hope. How to remedy the misguided policy of disregarding property rights is what the British business community should pay attention to today. It seems that our financial industry should also have considerable preparations for this. If our banking industry is only focused on maintaining strength and has no concrete countermeasures, I am afraid that national industries will have less and less protection in the future.

Yin Deyang Discusses the Recent Situation of the Hunan-Hubei Railway

The Ministry of Railways is currently borrowing 3 million yuan from the Boxer Indemnity Fund. 300,000 sleepers will be replaced before June of this year, and the entire line will be replaced before June of next year. At the end of last year, in addition to matching revenue and expenditure, the total annual surplus was approximately 370,000 yuan. The Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section of the project is currently being handled by Director Ling Hongxun and is expected to be open to traffic around January of the 25th year. In addition, a meeting of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, Hunan-Hubei Railway, and Zhuzhou-Shaoguan Railway bureaus will be held in Guangzhou on March 15 to discuss ways to improve the railway. Ministry of Industry Allocates Funds to Subsidize Afforestation Programs in Three Provinces

[Nanjing] The Ministry of Industry believes that the Yellow River dike is often in danger of collapsing, and the fundamental solution is to plant trees along the river. It previously notified the provinces of Gansu, Suiyuan, and Shaanxi to formulate concrete implementation plans for afforestation along the river, and it intends to allocate 20,000 yuan from the Ministry's 23rd fiscal year first reserve fund to subsidize Gansu, Suiyuan, and Shaanxi to implement the original plan and measures for afforestation along the river. The measures have been approved by the Yuan's meeting: (1) Allocate 20,000 yuan for afforestation in the upper reaches of the Yellow River, with 18,000 yuan distributed equally among the three provinces and 2,000 yuan for supervision expenses; (2) The subsidized provinces must provide more than three times the amount of the subsidy for afforestation expenses; (3) After the provincial funding is determined, the Ministry of Industry will send a supervisor to cooperate with the forestry authorities of each province to plan the afforestation; (4) This afforestation will be based on requisitioning labor in principle, and the above-mentioned funds will not cover administrative or labor costs. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Three District Bureaus of the Jiangsu Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Bureau to Be Managed by the Department of Finance

Jiangsu Provincial Government Approves Regulations for Collecting House Tax in Various Counties

[Zhenjiang] The Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee resolved on the 26th to approve the regulations for collecting house tax in various counties of Jiangsu Province, as well as the provisional measures for accommodating drug offenders sentenced by military law institutions in new and old prisons. The measures for collecting house tax are as follows: all counties in Jiangsu, whether they have implemented a house tax or not, will uniformly collect a house tax, divided into shop houses and residential houses. The tax rate for shop houses is 15% of the monthly rent, and for residential houses it is 8%. For self-produced shops, the property value will be estimated, with a tax of 1.5 yuan per 1,000 yuan. The tax rate for residential houses is 8 jiao per 1,000 yuan, and the same applies to mortgaged properties. The house tax for shop houses will be borne equally by the landlord and the tenant, while the tax for residential houses will be borne solely by the landlord. Houses with a rent of less than 2 yuan are exempt. The house tax will be paid monthly by the tenants. A surcharge of 10% will be added for payments overdue by 10 days, 20% for 20 days, 30% for 30 days, and 50% for two months. The regulations will be implemented starting from March 1st and will be handled by the tax collection offices of each county. It is reported that the collection of house tax in Jiangsu Province this time is not to increase the burden on the people. The public security expenses of various counties mostly come from the house tax, which is collected by the public security organs themselves. The tax rates also vary greatly. In order to reorganize the public security expenses of various counties, these unified measures have been formulated to standardize the tax rates and ensure uniformity. (26th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Personnel of the Baoding Headquarters to Change Date of Departure for Beijing

[Beiping] Baoding News: After the Headquarters received the order to close, all personnel, officials, and soldiers will change their departure date for Beijing to the end of the month. All case files and documents will be loaded onto the train and transported south. (26th Special Dispatch)

Amidst Pro-China Sentiments, Japan Worries About British and American Actions

Foreign Ministry Issues Unofficial Statement

Says the Principle of the Premier and the Hirota Policy Coincide

East Asian Peace Hinges on Sino-Russian Understanding of Japan

[Tokyo] Most European and American countries are jealous of the improvement in Sino-Japanese relations and are devising various strategies. The Foreign Ministry made the following unofficial statement on the 25th: (1) The reason why China has recently understood Japan's China policy is that the fundamental policy of the National Government, the Great Asiaism of Premier Sun, completely coincides with the East Asiaism advocated by Foreign Minister Hirota. (2) When the Manchurian Incident occurred, the attitude of the United Kingdom and the United States in attacking Japan was that it was disrupting the peace of East Asia and even the peace of the world. They asserted that there was no way to solve the Far East problem except to establish friendly relations between China and Japan. Today, seeing that Sino-Japanese relations have improved, they are making statements and actions to obstruct them, even advocating Anglo-American cooperation, which is ridiculous. It seems that what the United Kingdom and the United States truly hope for in East Asia is to disrupt peace and prevent Sino-Japanese friendship. Therefore, the East Asia policy of the United Kingdom and the United States can be said to have exposed its true colors, etc. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

[Tokyo] A Japanese Upper House member questioned the foreign policy yesterday, saying that the United States is the least understanding of Japan on the issue of the disarmament conference. Why doesn't the Foreign Minister reach an agreement with the United States first, so that diplomatic peace can be hoped for, and replace it with the five-nation treaty of Japan, the United States, France, Italy, and the United Kingdom? The Foreign Minister said that the United Kingdom and the United States are equally unable to understand Japan's position on the disarmament issue, and it is impossible to distinguish who is easier or more difficult. Japan is not afraid of the United Kingdom and the United States not understanding Japan, and only seeks that the two major neighboring countries, China and Russia, can understand Japan. China's attitude towards Japan has made great progress, and Russia is also gradually understanding Japan. The issue of the purchase of the Chinese Eastern Railway has been resolved. Japan plans to further resolve outstanding issues with Russia. It is reported that the Japanese Foreign Ministry plans to resolve the following issues with Russia as soon as possible: (1) The Japan-Russia Fisheries Treaty, (2) The issue of the exchange rate of Japanese and Russian currencies, (3) The border issue between Japan, Russia, and "Manchukuo." Regarding the first and second issues, the Japanese side proposed convening a conference in Tokyo to revise the Fisheries Treaty, and the Russian side has already accepted its principle, but the Russian side's instructions on the location of the meeting have not yet arrived. (26th China United Press Dispatch)

Wang Chonghui Discusses Concrete Plans with Hirota Yesterday to Enhance Sino-Japanese Relations

Cooperation Between the Two Countries Must Be Based on Equality

Wang Changes Date to Leave Japan for Europe on the 5th of Next Month

[Tokyo] Because Dr. Wang Chonghui has many people to talk to, he has postponed his departure from Japan. Wang was originally scheduled to take the President Coolidge to the United States on March 1st, but now he plans to take the Empress of Canada instead. His departure date is approximately March 5th. This morning, Wang and Hirota and Shigemitsu held talks for about an hour and a half. In the afternoon, he visited Army Vice Chief of Staff General Sugiyama. He plans to visit Hakone tomorrow. According to the Kokumin Shimbun, Wang discussed concrete plans with Foreign Minister Hirota to enhance Sino-Japanese friendship. According to Wang, he feels that Hirota's views on Sino-Japanese cooperation completely coincide with his own. Wang told Hirota that Japan must abandon its self-elevated attitude, because enhancing relations between the two countries must be based on equality, etc. (26th Reuters Dispatch)

[Tokyo] Wang Chonghui visited Foreign Minister Hirota on the 26th to express his farewell and expressed his gratitude to all aspects of the government and the public. The following is a transcript of his conversation:

The impression I received from the Japanese government and the public this time can be summed up in the word "excellent." I am very pleased that I have been able to convey the true intentions of the Chinese people to various important figures in your country. At the same time, I am confident that I have been able to fully convey the true intentions of your country to the Chinese people. China and Japan, in accordance with their historical destiny, are aware of their responsibility as fundamentally and substantially responsible for peace, and trust each other to realize equal and mutually beneficial cooperation on the basis of friendship and understanding, and contribute to the establishment of world peace. This belief is deeply rooted in the minds of the people of China and Japan. On this point, I have been able to achieve half of the purpose of my visit to Japan this time, and I should thank the gentlemen from all aspects of your country for their efforts and kindness. I also hope that your Excellency will continue to assist in the establishment of Sino-Japanese cooperation on the basis of this friendship and understanding in the future.

After Foreign Minister Hirota expressed the above views to Wang, he also said that the feelings that the Japanese government and the public have expressed to Wang this time are also the feelings of the entire Japanese people towards China. The concrete foundation for friendly cooperation between the two countries is strongly advocated to be established on this occasion, and Wang's efforts this time are praised. It is also hoped that he will come out and assist in the future. After visiting the Foreign Minister, Wang visited Vice President of the Privy Council Hiranuma and former Foreign Minister Yoshizawa on the same afternoon, and they exchanged frank opinions with each other. (26th Japan United Press Dispatch)

[Tokyo] Wang Chonghui is scheduled to leave Tokyo for Hakone on the morning of the 27th and stay at the Fuji Hotel. Because Wang hopes to visit Nikko and its scenic spots, he has decided to postpone his departure until March 5th and change to the Empress of Canada ship. (26th Japan United Press Dispatch)

[Tokyo] On the evening of the 19th, Wang Chonghui met his old friend Wu Zhenlin on the evening of his arrival in Tokyo. Wang and Wu were classmates at Cambridge University in the United Kingdom and were both Chinese diplomats. Wu married the niece of Japanese House of Peers member Izawa Takio and served as Acting Minister to Japan and Minister to Peru. Later, he resigned due to an incident. His wife died of illness, and he went to Japan to live his impoverished life. Hearing about his recent situation on Wang's visit to Japan this time, he immediately invited him to the Imperial Hotel and advised him to take up a government post again and do his best for Sino-Japanese friendship. (26th Japan United Press Dispatch)

Promoting Sales of Woolen Textiles

Nagoya: Aichi Prefecture produces 120 million yen worth of woolen textiles every year, most of which are shipped to overseas markets to compete with foreign goods. Simon Decides to Visit Berlin to Hold Direct Talks with Germany and Britain

Further Discussion of the London Declaration

Whether to Go to Moscow Awaits Cabinet Decision

[London] Foreign Secretary Simon recently stated in the House of Commons, "I hope to go to Berlin in the shortest possible time. As for the question of whether to go to Moscow and Warsaw, it is currently under study." Simon also said, "The German government's proposal for direct talks between Britain and Germany has been accepted in principle by the British government." The Labour leader in the House of Commons, Lansbury, immediately asked whether the government had already made any statement regarding the German proposal. Simon replied, "Yes, after receiving the German proposal, the British government inquired of the German government whether the direct talks between Britain and Germany mentioned in the German communication could include a further discussion of the issues raised in the Anglo-French declaration of February 3. Subsequently, I received a reply from Germany confirming this interpretation. Based on this foundation, I was invited to go to Berlin. The British government believes that this German proposal is very beneficial, so it hopes that I will go to Berlin as soon as possible. The date has yet to be decided, and the detailed procedures for this trip are still being prepared. The governments of France and Italy have both approved this plan." (Havas, 20th)

[London] Although Foreign Secretary Simon's statement in the House of Commons today was reserved regarding the trip to Russia, it is generally believed that after Simon and Lord Privy Seal Eden go to Berlin, they will probably go to Moscow, or perhaps even to Warsaw. If important results are achieved in the Berlin talks, Simon and Eden may temporarily return to Britain and then go directly from Britain to Russia and Poland. The British government believes that if the countries cannot conclude a general mutual assistance treaty, then it is necessary for the security to consolidate and strengthen the existing diplomatic constraints between the Eastern European countries. Therefore, it is essential for British cabinet members to visit Russia and Poland. (Havas, 25th)

[London] The Times reports that the decision on whether Foreign Secretary Simon will make a trip to Moscow after visiting Berlin will be made at tomorrow's cabinet meeting. Some cabinet members believe that Simon should return to the country upon leaving Berlin, and at the same time, the British ambassadors to Poland and the Soviet Union should consult with the governments of those countries on the issue of an Eastern European mutual assistance pact to ascertain whether it is necessary for the Foreign Secretary to go to Moscow. (Havas, 26th)

The Austrian authorities, therefore, have a more secure belief in the country's future." "L'Écho de Paris" reports that the Danube River Convention will inevitably be the target of the talks during Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to Berlin, and issues such as the air mutual assistance pact, disarmament, a general convention, and Germany's return to the League of Nations will also be discussed. As for the "North-Eastern European mutual assistance pact, it will be reserved and not discussed, and the French and German authorities will continue to consult in order to seek a solution." Famous French Journalist Doubts British Attitude

[Paris] Today, the famous French diplomatic and political journalist, Bodinart, published an article in "L'Écho de Paris," expressing indignation at British Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to Berlin and direct negotiations with Germany. According to Bodinart's prediction, after the British Foreign Secretary arrives in Germany, he will grant Germany certain concessions that France will find difficult to accept. Bodinart pointed to the British Foreign Secretary's attitude as belonging to the "unstable" side, and as for what he called a certain concession, he said that future local treaties will inevitably lose the components of mutual assistance and military agreements, and these components are indispensable to the agreements currently under discussion. Purpose of Austrian Chancellor's Visit to Britain

Seeking Financial and Military Assistance

To Resist German Influence from Moving East

[London] Austrian Foreign Minister Weidegger stated today that if Germany and Austria want to maintain friendly relations, the National Socialist Party must stop interfering in Austrian affairs. Weidegger made this statement during a special interview with the Associated Press reporter after arriving here. Weidegger also said, "Austria's independence has been confirmed, so we are not afraid of Germany interfering in Austrian affairs again. As for the friendly relations between the two countries, they can only be restored if the German authorities abandon all demands on Austria. In the future, unless Austria is recognized as an equal and independent country, we will not be willing to discuss Austrian affairs again. However, if a meeting is held based on this principle to solve diplomatic difficulties, we would be happy to participate. If Germany accepts this case, we would also be very happy to restore normal relations." It is widely rumored here that the real purpose of Schuschnigg and Weidegger's visit to Britain is to get Britain to allow the restoration of the Habsburg monarchy. According to the official announcement of the nature of the meeting, Austria requested Britain to allow assistance to the Austrian government to resist the forces of the National Socialist Party and the Communist Party, and to provide financial or military assistance when necessary. Another theory is that Schuschnigg's trip is to raise a loan in England, so he is scheduled to meet with the Governor of the Bank of England, Norman, once. Semi-official sources have paid close attention to Weidegger's aforementioned remarks. It is said that it can be seen from this that the Austrian political system will not be changed. (National News Agency, 26th)

British-Austrian Talks Largely the Same as Paris Talks

Restoration and Loan Issues Not Mentioned

[London] The issues discussed in the British-Austrian talks are completely consistent with those discussed in the Paris talks. The results obtained are also largely the same as the results of the Franco-Austrian talks, that is, to recognize that the Austrian Republic should maintain complete independence in all respects. Today, Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg, Foreign Minister Weidegger, British Foreign Secretary Simon, and Permanent Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs Vansittart held talks, which lasted a long time. The main part of the talks was about the treaty on non-interference in Austrian internal affairs. According to the Austrian side, if Austria is subjected to foreign interference, the signatory countries can directly consult with Austria, and non-signatory countries can also consult with Austria through the mediation of the League of Nations. Although this British-Austrian talk is only exploratory in nature, it is actually very important. The Danube River Convention will be one of the main issues in the British-German Berlin talks. Now, before Foreign Secretary Simon goes to Germany, holding talks with Austrian cabinet members can clarify Austria's position, which is of great benefit. As for the issues of the restoration of the Habsburg monarchy, increasing Austrian loans, and the amount of the army, they were not mentioned at all in the British-Austrian talks. Although the Governor of the Bank of England, Norman, visited Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg today, what was discussed was about Austria's old loans, such as loans handled by the League of Nations. It is also generally believed that when Schuschnigg met with British Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain this afternoon, they discussed whether Britain could advance funds to enable Austria to purchase railway materials from Britain to renovate Austria's railway equipment. (Havas, 25th)

Austrian Chancellor Declares That Political System Will Not Be Changed

[London] Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg recently declared to representatives of the international press, "We do not adopt a dictatorship system because of building Austria. This kind of evolution is contrary to our nature. No one in our country wants it to be realized." Schuschnigg then talked about Austria's national strength, saying that if Austria can exchange what it has with foreign countries, it can survive independently without having to unite with other countries. (Havas, 26th)

US Navy Base Strengthens Strength Plan

Needs to Spend 38 Million Dollars

Approved by the House Naval Affairs Committee

[Washington] The House Naval Affairs Committee recently passed a bill with a majority of fourteen votes to one, authorizing the Navy Department to carry out a plan to strengthen US naval bases. The naval bases along the Canadian, Panamanian, and Pacific coasts must be strengthened, with a total cost of 38 million US dollars, of which 15 million US dollars will be used to build submarine and aviation bases at Pearl Harbor, Hawaii. (Havas, 25th)

[Washington] The House Naval Affairs Committee today approved an appropriation of US$38 million to rebuild the naval docks on the west coast of the United States, the Panama Canal Zone, and the Hawaiian Islands. The committee also approved that the Navy does not need to obtain special permission from Congress to double the funds for improving warships. According to existing regulations, the Navy does not need to request Congressional approval to improve any warship within two years if each ship does not exceed 300,000 yuan. Now the committee has approved this number to be increased to 600,000 yuan. As for the proposal to improve the docks, naval experts have long regarded it as very important. Some officials believe that the United States must prepare to build a large number of warships at any time. The lack of ships during the European War can be used as a lesson. Some experts said that after the government improves the docks, it can save waste, because national construction is cheaper than temporary bidding by merchants, but opinions on this point vary greatly. (National Telegram, 25th)

Italian War Fever

Troops Continuously Transported to East Africa

Italian-Ethiopian Negotiations at a Standstill

Messina The Italian government continues to plan a large-scale offensive against Abyssinia. Today, thousands of troops and countless war supplies departed from here again. The war sentiment throughout Italy has become white-hot. When the troops set off, tens of thousands of people went to the port to wave flags and send them off, and distributed flowers, cigarettes, sweets, and other things to comfort them. A ship carrying 1,200 engineers and a lot of military fire also left for East Africa. According to Italy, this time the dispatch of troops to Italian Somalia has reached more than 6,000 before and after, and there are still 10,000 people preparing to set off. At present, the responsibility of this army is only to assist the local 25,000 soldiers to protect the border and prevent disturbances in Ethiopia. Ethiopia has also concentrated 75,000 to 100,000 troops to wait for orders to attack. Ethiopian officials have repeatedly protested Italy's continued dispatch of heavy troops, pointing out that it is a provocative action. The League of Nations Committee, which is meeting in the Ethiopian capital, is also still trying to prevent the conflict between the two sides, but Ethiopia still deals with this matter with an indifferent attitude. The Ethiopian King still claims that he will rely on the League of Nations and his army to protect Ethiopia from Italian invasion. Therefore, it makes the Italian officials even more angry. Now Italy has ordered that merchant ships will be requisitioned for military use when necessary. From this, the urgency of war preparation has gone a step further. (National Telegram, 25th)

[Rome] The First Battalion of the Fascist Party Army, which left the port of Naples on February 10th on the Argentine postal ship to East Africa, has recently landed at the port of Massawa in Italian Eritrea. After being reorganized, they entered the city, and the people welcomed them along the way. The troops of the Belluno Division that have not yet set off have also left from the port of Messina for East Africa. Vice Minister of the Army Bestrocci went to Catania and Syracuse today to inspect the troops, and finally returned to Messina to inspect the troops waiting to board the ship. The "Count Biancamano" arrived in Messina this morning from the port of Naples, and will carry 2,600 soldiers and 3,000 tons of military equipment to East Africa. Bishop Benno of the port of Messina boarded the ship to deliver a farewell speech and bless the ship and its crew. When the ship set sail, the crowd on the shore cheered loudly. (Havas, 25th)

[Rome] The negotiations between Italy and Ethiopia have not yet resulted in any agreement. According to Italy's previous proposal to Ethiopia, a neutral zone should be set up six kilometers away from the outposts of the two countries to avoid conflicts between the two sides. Ethiopia has accepted this proposal, but with a condition that Ethiopian nomadic people should be allowed to pass freely through the neutral zone, because there are a number of springs in the neutral zone. This condition was also accepted by Italy, but Ethiopia's request that one Belgian and one Swedish officer each participate in the neutral zone demarcation delegation was rejected by Italy. According to some foreign sources, Ethiopia has now abandoned this request, but Rome has not received any news, only saying that this matter is being discussed in the Ethiopian capital, but whether there are any results is unknown. According to foreign sources, Ethiopia requested submission to arbitration, but Italy did not respond. People here say that Ethiopia's note requesting submission to arbitration was only delivered on February 23, and Italy is now drafting a reply. Italy's opinion is that the solution to the dispute between the two countries should be divided into three steps: first, direct negotiations, if they fail, then mediation by a third country, and if mediation fails again, then submission to arbitration. Now that Italy and Ethiopia have begun direct negotiations in the Ethiopian capital, there is of course no talk of arbitration. (Havas, 25th)

To Thank Them for Handling the Saar Issue Fairly

[Berlin] German leader Hitler today invited the three-member Saar Commission of the League of Nations to tour Germany in order to personally thank them for handling the Saar issue with a fair attitude. (Reuters, 25th)

Saarbrücken Today, the Saar Governing Commission issued a bulletin, disclosing the full text of the Saar Transfer Agreement, stating that the Saar region will be returned to Germany at midnight on February 28, and an agreement has been concluded between the Commission and Germany, which stipulates that all the Commission's assets and debts, as well as the existing debts and liabilities, will be taken over by Germany and continue to be assumed. (National Telegram, 25th)

Gran Chaco Triangle Land, Bolivia and Paraguay Fight to Death

Ceasefire Deadline Expired Yesterday

Paraguay's Tyranny Is Despised by the World

[Washington] Paraguay today insisted on continuing the war in the uninhabited area, leading to its being despised by the world and denounced as a tyrannical country. Today is the expiration date of the three-month ceasefire between Bolivia and Paraguay. The League of Nations' ruling will not be in Paraguay's favor, but Paraguayan officials have heard in advance that member states of the League of Nations may adopt severe sanctions, so they withdrew from the League of Nations on Saturday night. At the same time, it is learned that the two countries will continue to engage in sporadic local battles in the Gran Chaco. The Gran Chaco War originated in 1879. Its position is between the Paraguay and Pilcomayo rivers, with waterways intersecting. It is a large triangular area filled with insects, 600 miles long and 300 miles wide. Bolivia and Paraguay each demand the land for their own reasons. The land is regarded by landlocked Bolivia as the only way to the sea. Although Bolivia is only 75 miles from the Pacific Ocean, it is impossible to reach it due to heavy mountains. Paraguay is also eyeing the land covetously, because its large area will actually double the area of Paraguay's land. Moreover, there are many plants in the wilderness, and their bark can be used to extract 30% of the bark quality. In 1932, representatives of nineteen countries gathered in Washington to discuss ways to resolve the dispute. At that time, 10,000 soldiers had sacrificed their lives in the war. Later, the issue was transferred to the League of Nations for handling. The League of Nations notified both sides that the war must end as soon as yesterday. Paraguay's withdrawal from the League is the reply to the League of Nations' notification. (National Telegram, 25th)

[Geneva] Paraguay has announced its withdrawal from the League due to dissatisfaction with the League's attitude. The Consultative Committee established by the League of Nations to resolve the dispute between Paraguay and Bolivia over the Gran Chaco will probably hold a meeting soon to discuss the situation caused by Paraguay's withdrawal and study how to continue the League's appeasement work. (Havas, 26th)

France Supports US Proposal on Arms Supervision

Britain and Italy Still Oppose

[Geneva] The US representative of the Disarmament Conference Committee has now decided to proceed with its proposal to establish a permanent League of Nations Committee to manage arms trade. US representative Wilson made this statement today, saying that he will amend the original US proposal to give the Permanent Committee the power to supervise and manage on the spot. In this way, the Committee can inspect factories that manufacture military fire, but the exercise of management power must take into account national feelings and must not become a source of conflict. Britain and Italy are currently opposing this proposal, believing that the US proposal is too broad and difficult to implement, while France supports the US position. (Reuters, 25th)

Suspicion of Sabotage in the Crash of the American Airship

Prominent Engineer's Unique Observation

No Less Than a Massive Bombshell to the Investigative Committee

[Washington] The world-renowned airship engineer, Mr. Knabenshue, stated today to the House Licensing Committee that the reason for the crash of the airship Macon was that someone sabotaged the machinery. Mr. Knabenshue's declaration was nothing short of throwing a massive bombshell at the committee. However, the ship's captain, Mr. Wiley, declared that this was impossible. Thus, public sentiment seems to have calmed down compared to before. Mr. Knabenshue has been retired for several years, so he did not want to exaggerate his words, saying that the Macon was deliberately sabotaged. Mr. Knabenshue declared that if the process of the accident could be investigated, then you will be able to find that sabotaging the machinery was a major cause of the accident, and that the sabotage work may have been carried out during the airship's voyage. In response to the question of whether foreign governments were related to the accident, Mr. Knabenshue said, "I must beg to be excused from answering." Knabenshue explained that he did not believe that naval officers were involved in the conspiracy to sabotage the airship, and said that he respected American officers, so he did not believe they would resort to such a low tactic. He asked the committee and Congress to continue to adopt airships as a tool of national defense, especially in defending the West Coast. Captain Wiley, after hearing Mr. Knabenshue's statement, expressed his opinion, saying, "I do not believe that this accident was related to sabotaging the machinery. We always set up heavy guards around the suspension bridge of the Macon, and patrolled the entire ship according to the prescribed time. I believe it is even more impossible to carry out sabotage work during the airship's voyage." It is said that all seventy-three crew members on the Macon knew that they could not escape after the airship crashed. Therefore, it is doubtful whether there were spies mixed in who were willing to sacrifice their lives to carry out sabotage work. (Twenty-fifth National Telegram)

Four Hundred and Thirty Thousand Survivors Still Exist

A Bloody Human Leg Found in a Train Car

A Bizarre Murder Case in England

[London] After a British Kingston district train arrived at Waterloo Station today, a cleaner discovered a package wrapped in brown paper under a seat. Its weight and shape were quite suspicious. The cleaner immediately took the original package to the lost luggage room. The railway police opened it and were shocked to find a pair of human legs, cut off from the knees, seemingly cut off only a few hours ago. The railway police were extremely frightened and immediately reported to the police station by telephone. Police officers rushed to inspect the scene and dispatched personnel to the 26 stations passed by the train to begin an investigation, hoping to solve this bizarre murder case as soon as possible. Now, the only clue available for research is this pair of male legs. The case is being handled by Police Chief Donaldson, who also handled the Brighton Trunk Murder Case. Circumstances of Yang Jianping's Arrest in Hong Kong

Yang Was Still in a Dream When Arrested Preliminary Hearing in Primary Court

Hong Kong Correspondence, Yang Jianping, the former Director of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, was a confidant of Chen Mingshu. When Chen was in power, he was extremely popular. Yang was also able to understand Chen's intentions, so he was able to follow Chen everywhere and be appointed to high positions. When Chen established a pseudo-People's Government in Fuzhou two years ago, Yang was also appointed as a member of the Economic Committee. When the Fujian affair failed, Yang fled to Hong Kong with Chen. His private residence was on the second floor of No. 46, Village Road, Happy Valley. He was suddenly arrested by Hong Kong detectives at midnight on the 20th. The details are as follows:

It is reported that when Yang was the Director of the Shanghai Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, he embezzled 34,000 yuan of public funds and hid in Hong Kong. Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Government sent a document to Hong Kong requesting that Yang be detained and extradited to Shanghai for interrogation. The Hong Kong police authorities then ordered an investigation and learned that Yang lived on Village Road, Happy Valley. Therefore, English detective Mr. Murdoch, accompanied by several Chinese detectives, went to Yang's residence at midnight on the 20th and arrested Yang back to the station. When the detectives arrived at Yang's residence, Yang was still in a dream. After the detectives explained their intentions and showed the arrest warrant, Yang put on his suit and followed them to the police station.

After arresting Yang, the police authorities immediately prepared a document to the primary court accusing Yang of embezzling 34,000 yuan of public funds from the Shanghai Postal Savings Bureau. The case was handled by Judge Smith. At 11 a.m. that morning, Yang was brought to court. The government was prosecuted by Deputy Attorney General Fraser. Yang's legal advisor, Xian Wenlian, requested lawyers Zeng Jian and Luo Xiansheng to represent Yang in court. Lawyer Zeng first requested that the defendant be allowed to post bail, saying that the defendant should be allowed, but if not allowed, he would state his reasons. The prosecutor said that he did not absolutely oppose bail, but wanted to hear the reasons. Lawyer Zeng said that he had just read the arrest warrant, which stated that about two and a half years ago, the defendant worked in a government agency and embezzled 34,000 yuan of public funds. The defendant has been living in Hong Kong for a long time, and has not left Hong Kong for even a step in the recent six months. And a few months ago, the defendant had already notified the police station through his legal advisor that whenever someone arrested him, he was always prepared to go to the station to surrender. Under these circumstances, the defendant has no chance to escape. Therefore, based on these reasons, he wanted to ask the judge to allow him to post a fair amount of bail. He also said that the defendant has no property in Hong Kong, only cash in the bank. After listening, Judge Smith asked Lawyer Zeng, "Can he find two guarantors?" Lawyer Zeng said, "He is willing to use cash as collateral because he does not want to involve others." Judge Smith said, "Considering the amount of embezzlement, I think a guarantee of 50,000 yuan is the fairest." Attorney Fraser said that the Chinese government requested his extradition, and there was a treaty between them. This case is not an ordinary criminal case and should be handled with caution. He then cited precedents, saying that according to the bail precedents, the judge could allow bail in this case, but the bench did not absolutely oppose the bail, but opposed the cash bail. Fraser then cited the British extradition precedents to express his personal opinion, saying that if only cash bail was used, it should not be allowed. Now that the fugitive has been brought to court, the judge should be especially careful. For the sake of strict prevention, the bench advocated that two people (jointly or separately guaranteeing) should be attached with a security deposit. Lawyer Zeng said that it was difficult to find a guarantor, and his client was prepared to provide 50,000 yuan in cash as collateral, and that 50,000 yuan was already too much for such a common accusation. Judge Smith said, "That is true, but we must also consider strictly abiding by the treaty. Therefore, I believe that without finding two guarantors, bail cannot be allowed." Lawyer Zeng said, "That is true for ordinary extradition cases, but this case has special circumstances and cannot be compared. The Nanjing government must be aware of the whereabouts of its officials. How could it not know about the defendant's trip to the south? If he was really guilty, he would not have been allowed to live in Hong Kong and would not have dared to surrender himself to the police, and would have left Hong Kong long ago. This kind of fact is very excusable." Judge Smith said, "I will ultimately not allow a simple cash guarantee. Two people are required as guarantors." He then ordered the case to be adjourned for a week. At this point, Yang Jianping said the names of several guarantors, entrusting lawyers Xi and Luo to solicit opinions from everyone. Among those mentioned by Yang were Hu Hanmin, Chen Mingshu, Zou Minchu, Deng Ruiren and others in the political circles, and two Hong Kong gentlemen in the business circles. However, because that day was a race day, they went to the races and it was not easy to visit everyone for a while, and the court also stopped working in the afternoon, so Yang was detained, and it was learned that the police authorities had immediately reported the case to the Shanghai authorities. (February 21)

Songjiang

Farmer surnamed Xue Robbed

Dahai Sixteen Township, Seventh District, Punan, the home of Xue Yunzhang, a villager, was suddenly visited by more than ten bandits last night (25th). Each had their faces painted with white powder and spoke local dialects. The leader held a box cannon and commanded the group. The rest held wooden sticks, iron rulers, ropes, etc. After entering the door, the victim woke up from his dream and was forced to hand over silver by the victim's mother, Mrs. Xue. She had nothing to give, begging for mercy. The bandits signed that you have a surplus, and it is useless to deny it. They then bound Xue's limbs, hung her in the side room, and her screams were not answered. While the bandits were smashing the cabinets and boxes, the neighbors heard something and quickly rang the gong to gather the crowd. The bandits did not dare to stay and fled in all directions. Although Mrs. Xue suffered no losses, her body has been severely injured. According to the mid-December of last year, the Xue family was also robbed, and they were also dispersed by the neighbors ringing gongs. There were no losses. However, the bandits paid attention to the Xue family, which was probably done by familiar bandits. It is said that the Xue family did have savings in the past and has already distributed them to their children.

If the cloudy and rainy weather continues, the harvest of soybeans and wheat may be hopeless, and there are many worries about the future of the people.

According to reports, the provincial government considers opium prohibition to be the central task of the year. Many opium addicts in various counties have not yet been registered. Therefore, a self-surrender program is being organized for opium offenders, along with public awareness campaigns. On one hand, the Baojia system is being used to investigate and encourage opium offenders to surrender themselves. On the other hand, propaganda can be conducted in schools to make elementary school students aware that opium addiction is a shameful act. The current county opium rehabilitation centers are treating opium addicts. After the work is completed, the province plans to convert them into county hospitals. Regarding recent reports of abolishing or merging retail shops and rehabilitation centers, the province is still in the planning stage and cannot express its opinion. On the 25th, Commissioner Qin participated in the county opium prohibition association's publicity week for opium offenders to surrender themselves, staying for about two days before going to Wuxian, Kunshan, and Wujiang counties for inspection.

Hefei

Large Number of Prisoners Escape

Over a thousand bandits are currently gathered in the Wenji and Huangtongmiao areas on the border of Hefei and Chaoxian counties, looting everywhere and posing a serious threat. The newly appointed County Magistrate Zhao Xiaosan has dispatched the 1st, 2nd, 3rd, 4th, and 5th Security Squads to intercept and suppress them, while also telegraphing the province to request military assistance. Unexpectedly, at around 2:00 PM on the 20th, taking advantage of the weak city defenses, eleven prisoners from the county jail, including Liu Dapao, Xia Bangyi, and Cai Qingbing, seized the guards' guns and escaped, heading west. Prison Warden Lü Yong immediately reported to the county government, which dispatched the 6th Security Squad to pursue them. Four were killed outside the west gate, and Wei Shengdou was captured. Six remain at large and are currently being actively searched for. By 6:00 PM, Ren's battalion of the 11th Route Army had arrived in Hefei from the province and was stationed inside and outside the city, greatly reassuring the public. The Wuhu Special Office and the Chaoxian County Government have also received orders from the province to dispatch teams to jointly suppress the eastern bandits. It is expected that they will be eradicated soon.

Special Dispatch

Discussing Whether to Build Salt Warehouses on the Gan River at Jiujiang and Hukou; It is Better to Build Them at Jiujiang and Wucheng. (Continued)

— Yu Zhongbiao

3. Advantages of Building Warehouses in Wucheng

Wucheng is suitable for building warehouses and depots due to historical, geographical, and other factors, which can be explained in five points as follows:

(1) Advantage in terms of transportation and sales. Wucheng is the confluence of the rivers in Gan Province, as mentioned above, especially convenient for Xiushui, Tonggu, Wuning, Fengxin, Jing'an, and Anyi counties. If warehouses are built here, the sailing transport from the above counties will not incur the cost of setting up stations midway, and there is the advantage of direct access by sail. This is beneficial to both merchants and navigation, far superior to Hukou. However, some argue: "Sailing transport cannot risk reaching Hukou, while Jianglun can uniquely navigate shallow waters to Wucheng. Commercial transport cannot set up stations midway, while official shipping can uniquely transfer cargo along the river? This is convenient for private interests but not for public interests, which is a one-sided view." It is not known that the government is actively dredging waterways. For example, the Fu River has been instructed by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to be planned by the Jiangxi Provincial Government, assigning counties along the river to dredge. Poyang Lake is specified in the General's Founding Strategy; how can it be allowed to silt up? However, the project is larger, and the time is slower. After the dredging, Jianglun will be able to reach Nanchang directly, let alone Wucheng. Even currently, Jianglun cannot directly sail to Wucheng only when the water level drops in autumn and winter. If the river water overflows in spring and summer, it is unimpeded. In the future, before the waterway is dredged, utilizing the spring and summer water to pre-store salt for autumn and winter will also be beneficial to both public and private interests?

(2) Advantage in terms of warehouse construction costs. Wucheng has historically been a river port in Jiangxi, so salt warehouses are numerous. In the future, the government will rent or buy them. If they are old, they will be repaired. If they are insufficient, they will be expanded. In my opinion, old salt merchants would not sit idly by and let them collapse. In this way, half the cost can build a warehouse, and half the effort can achieve twice the result. Compared to the cost of quarrying stones and filling depressions in Hukou to build from scratch, how much labor and cost can be saved?

(3) Advantage in terms of terrain security. Wucheng is located in central Gan, surrounded by water on all sides, purely a commercial port. In terms of security, it is truly unmatched by any place in Jiangxi. Evidence shows that in recent years, red bandits have ravaged the entire province. More than eighty counties have no pure land, but Wucheng remains aloof from the world, like a paradise. Merchants and travelers sleep peacefully, and chickens and dogs are not alarmed, which is sufficient evidence. If warehouses are built here to store salt, there will be no need for guards or treasures. It will be like having a city without walls, and a natural barrier without danger. No gold-encrusted city could surpass this.

(4) Advantage in terms of promoting local products. Major local products of Jiangxi, such as paper, hemp, and wood, are traditionally concentrated in Wucheng. Moreover, paper and hemp are produced in northern Gan (and a significant amount of timber). They are sold in the Yangtze River area. Often, sailboats transport local products to Wucheng and return fully loaded with salt. Wheel transport salt to Wucheng and then transfer it to paper and hemp. (In recent years, timber has also been transported out of the river by ships.) The wheel and sail transport does not go empty-handed. This benefits boatmen and promotes industry. At this time when bandits are being suppressed and all industries are declining, we are urgently seeking post-disaster reconstruction. Everything that can benefit the people's livelihood should be vigorously supported so that the people can ascend to prosperity early and eliminate banditry forever.

(5) Advantage in terms of workers' livelihood. Tens of thousands of people in Wucheng rely on salt directly or indirectly for their livelihood. If the warehouse is moved to Hukou, these tens of thousands of people will lose their livelihood at a time of high living costs. The weak will inevitably starve, and the cunning will embark on dangerous paths. The government is already in a state of starvation and drowning; how can it bear to do this? However, some argue: "Building warehouses in Hukou also requires workers. If you cannot bear the loss of livelihood of workers in Wucheng, do you only wish for the workers in Hukou to be on the verge of unemployment?" This is not the case. Hukou has no salt, but workers in Hukou may not be without food. It is merely "icing on the cake." If the warehouse is removed from Wucheng, the clothing and food of the workers in Wucheng will truly go with the salt. Why provide food after starvation, when it is better for everyone to get their food? Although the government is vigorously implementing streamlined sailing transport, according to the guidelines for salt transport passed by the Executive Yuan, there are provisions for opening paper mills, introducing employment, and immigrating workers for the drawn boatmen. This shows the government's concern for workers.

4. Conclusion

Based on the above arguments, the convenience of transportation and sales, the cost of expenses, and the safety of the terrain are most important. Even for the remaining points, although they are inferred by the author, national policies are of great importance. If possible, a comprehensive calculation should be made. The ability to make foolproof plans can benefit future generations. The author was born and raised here, and the advantages and disadvantages are clearer. If the authorities' plan to build warehouses in Hukou is out of expediency and still needs further consideration, then I hope they will pay attention to my humble opinion. (End)

Local News

Hongkong and Shanghai Bank Auctioned Shen Xin No. 7 Factory Yesterday

Ignoring the First Special Court's Provisional Attachment

Taken Over by Japanese Toyota Spinning Mill

According to the Central News Agency, the Shen Xin Textile Company's No. 7 Factory at 468 Yangshupu Road, valued at approximately 5 million yuan, was mortgaged to the British Hongkong and Shanghai Bank for 2 million yuan seven years ago, with an annual interest rate of 8%, resulting in an annual interest payment of 160,000 yuan. Over the seven years, the accumulated interest reached a staggering 1.12 million yuan. Upon maturity, due to the decline in the textile industry, the debt could not be repaid. Although Shen Xin was willing to repay part of the principal and all the interest and repeatedly negotiated with the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank, the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank resolutely entrusted the law firm of Lu Yishi & Mouyang to announce the auction at 3:30 PM yesterday at the bank's location at the intersection of Beijing Road and Sichuan Road. The factory land, buildings, and machinery were auctioned off for a limited price of 2.25 million yuan. However, the factory had been provisionally attached by the China Shanghai Two Banks, the second creditor, in the morning, so this auction was naturally without legal basis. The details of the auction and the responses from all parties are as follows:

History of Factory No. 7 According to the Guowen News Agency, Shen Xin No. 7 Factory originally belonged to a Japanese company called the Oriental Spinning Mill. Later, because the Japanese had no intention of operating it, Rong Zongjing purchased it for 1.8 million taels nine years ago. Due to the old machinery and spindles inside, it was improved several times, and the cost has reached more than 1 million yuan to date. In the past, when Yangshupu Road was still remote and land prices were quite low, someone once discussed with Rong to sell the land for 60,000 yuan per mu to be used for other purposes, but Rong did not agree. From this, it can be seen that the land alone is worth more than 3 million yuan. Today, it is sold for only 2.25 million yuan, which is extremely cheap.

Unsuccessful Prevention According to the Huadong News Agency, the authorities of the First Special District Court believed that the property rights had already been provisionally attached by the court, so the foreign firm had no right to auction it. Therefore, they sent personnel to prevent it yesterday, but the Lu Yishi & Mouyang law firm stated that the business was entrusted by the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank, so whether to auction it or not was up to the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank. However, the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank ignored the court's prevention and still ordered the foreign firm to auction it on its behalf. Therefore, at 3:30 PM yesterday, the auction still proceeded as scheduled.

Auction Details According to the Central News Agency, yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, a room in the Lu Yishi auction house on Beijing Road was crowded with Chinese and foreign men and women, as an unprecedented auction with a minimum value of 2.5 million was about to take place. At 3:30 PM, a Westerner from the auction house took the stage and read out the contract between Shen Xin and the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank for half an hour. At exactly 4:00 PM, the staff called out the minimum value of 2.25 million yuan, and two Japanese people in the crowd immediately responded that they were willing to purchase it for 2.25 million yuan. When the staff wanted to increase the price for auction, no one responded, so the hammer was struck, and the two Japanese lawyers, Murakami and Okamoto, were determined to be the buyers. When the Central News Agency reporter asked them on behalf of which company they were purchasing, they refused to announce it. Later, after investigation by the Central News Agency reporter, it was said that they were indeed representatives of the Japanese Toyota Spinning Mill. They then went to the office with the staff of the auction house and paid a deposit of 10,000 yuan.

Rumors of Buyers According to the investigation by a reporter from the Huadong News Agency, the winner of this bid was the Dalian Steamship Company, a Japanese company, which was purchased by the Toyota Textile Mill on its behalf. On the surface, it was taken over by the Japanese, but in reality, the Dalian Steamship Company planned to convert it into a pier. The Huangpu Pier of the Dalian Steamship Company at 340 Yangshupu Road is adjacent to the Shen Xin No. 7 Factory at 468 Yangshupu Road. The Shen Xin Factory is on the east, and the company's pier is on the west. The company has always coveted it, and now its wish has finally been fulfilled. It is reliably learned that the company will temporarily operate the Shen Xin No. 7 Factory as a textile mill in the near future, but it will soon be dismantled and rebuilt into a pier. Converted to 68 mu of land, each mu is only worth more than 30,000, and all the machinery and equipment are free of charge.

National Indignation According to the Central News Agency, the Chinese people present at the time were mostly aware that Shen Xin No. 7 Factory had been provisionally attached by the China Shanghai Two Banks, the second creditor of the factory, yesterday morning, and that this auction had lost its legal basis and would inevitably involve negotiations in the future. However, they all expressed indignation that such a huge industrial enterprise was announced for auction in the foreign auction house and was purchased by the Japanese at a low price.

Court's Statement A Central News Agency reporter immediately went to the First Special District Court to visit President Guo. Guo was out, so the Chief Clerk received the reporter. According to him, since the China Shanghai Two Banks, the second creditor of the factory, had already applied for provisional attachment, it would be handled in accordance with the law thereafter.

Opinions of the Yarn Industry According to the person in charge of the Yarn Factory Federation, it is a pity that Shen Xin No. 7 Factory was auctioned off by the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank. China's yarn factories have been on the verge of collapse for a long time due to the impact of the social depression and the dumping of Japanese yarn. Although manufacturers have struggled hard, they lack support. Although the banking industry intends to help, they are limited in their capacity. Although the auction has already taken place, they should still fight for it on the basis of reason to prevent the huge industry from falling into the hands of foreigners. He also said that President Wang recently sent a telegram, which may not have reached the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank before 3:30 to negotiate.

President Wang's Telegram (Omitted above) The telegram also stated that the court meeting today had decided to first persuade the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank by Shanghai Mayor Wu to postpone the auction and to consult with the Ministry of Finance and Industry to discuss relief measures. Separate telegrams have been sent. Special reply.

Rong's Conversation A Central News Agency reporter met with Rong Zongjing, General Manager of the company, at 5:00 PM. Lawyer Guo Shouyi represented him in the conversation, expressing opposition to the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank's auction of Factory No. 7. The China Shanghai Two Banks had promised to advance 1 million yuan to repay the debt, but it was still rejected by the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank. He also said that the various factories of the company pay more than 20,000 yuan in consolidated tax every day. After the shutdown of Factory No. 2 and Factory No. 5, the national tax revenue is reduced by 6,000 yuan per day, which is 180,000 yuan per month. If China's textile industry cannot be maintained, it will have an even greater impact on the country. The financial authorities had previously allowed the company's consolidated tax to be temporarily recorded on account, but in view of the national financial deficit, no points have been outstanding. In short, the financial authorities that collect the consolidated tax should provide relief to China's dying textile industry and prevent its collapse, which is an inescapable responsibility. As for future negotiations, the second creditor will be the focus.

General Labor Union's Telegram The city's General Labor Union telegraphed the central ministries yesterday, stating: To Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry, and Minister Wang, also Minister of Foreign Affairs, and Wang, Minister of the Ministry of Justice and Administration, the entire union of Shen Xin No. 7 Factory has reported that the factory was founded by industrialist Rong Zongjing, and the total assets are worth more than 5 million yuan. In recent years, due to the decline of the yarn industry and the inflexibility of economic turnover, the entire assets have been mortgaged to the British Hongkong and Shanghai Bank for a loan of 2 million yuan. Now, it is unable to repay the loan upon maturity and is willing to pay all the interest and raise a part of the principal. After repeated negotiations with the bank, it was not allowed. The bank suddenly announced on the 26th of this month to entrust Louis Smo to auction all the assets, which concerns the entire industry and the livelihood of all workers in China. Please give assistance and save the property rights and industry. Based on this, the Hongkong and Shanghai Bank, relying on its economic power, has arbitrarily disposed of the assets of Shen Xin No. 7 Factory, which is obviously intended to destroy China's industry. Therefore, please send an effective ban to save it, protect property rights, and maintain industry. The Shanghai General Labor Union bows.

Chamber of Commerce Petitions the Central Government to Exempt Trading Tax on Public Bonds

Stock Exchange is the Medium for Circulating National Debt

Should Generally be Exempted from Tax in Accordance with American and Japanese Precedents

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday presented a petition to the Central Political Conference, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance, stating the matter: On the 25th of this month, the Shanghai Chinese Stock Exchange and the brokerage association of the exchange jointly stated:

In a letter stating The proposal to levy a trading tax by the Ministry of Finance has prompted brokers from various exchanges in Shanghai to request the government to consider the concealment of merchants and to grant exemptions separately. Your association has filed a case on the basis of the situation, and our office is deeply grateful. However, the Legislative Yuan reviewed and revised the law, but no special exemption was offered for national bonds. The brokers of our office have repeatedly held meetings to discuss that if the government levies the same tax on public bond transactions as on ordinary company stocks, it will not only be meticulous and create an unprecedented precedent in the East and the West, but will also add restrictions to the promotion of national bonds at a time of economic difficulty. The harm to the national economy is unspeakable. According to the term trading tax, which originated in Europe and America and spread to Japan, the New York Stock Exchange in the United States in 1817 already had a prototype at No. 40 Wall Street. It was not officially established until 1863. The internal organization is large-scale, and all American railroad and bank stocks are considered to be the key to circulation. The government does its best to assist, so American economists have said that the foundation of the United States' financial stability is consolidated in the huge building on Broadway. Its support for the importance of the exchange is like this. In the Meiji year 20, Japan sent economic experts to Europe and the United States to study the exchange system, and followed suit. The organization of the exchange has been around for more than 30 years, and various laws have been completed. China's exchange law mostly adopts

Japanese precedents The Japanese Trading Tax Law was promulgated in March of the Taisho year 3. After several revisions, it was found to be difficult to implement. In April of the Taisho year 11, an amendment was promulgated. Article 5 of this law states that in the case of transactions on the exchange, the settlement of which is based on the payment of margin differences, the transaction tax shall be levied on the agreed amount of the transaction at the following tax rate. The so-called transaction tax is the transaction of the first type of local bonds or corporate bonds, the transaction of the second type of securities, the transaction of the third type of commodities. Article 7 states that the transaction of national bonds is not taxed. Japan's non-taxation of national bond transactions is a fixed article, and it is announced to the people. In addition, Article 15 of the Japanese Stock Exchange's Business Regulations, regarding long-term transactions of national bond tickets, does not levy a margin deposit on each broker who does not reach 10,000 yuan, but the exchange may levy it with the resolution of the board of directors when it deems it necessary. According to the transactions of the exchange, whether it is goods or securities, the margin is a necessary condition for the exchange to ensure the safety of both parties. Japan promotes the purchase and sale of national bonds.

To promote the purchase and sale Therefore, it does not hesitate to allow the exchange to take this risk and exempt the margin deposit, but it is also afraid that it is not safe, so it adds a proviso to save it. To sum up the two principles, Japan is doing its utmost to encourage the people to buy and sell national bond tickets, not to mention taxes. In addition, each country in the United States requires both parties to attach stamp tax to the sale and purchase of securities. The rules set by the New York Province of the United States also have a transfer tax, which is similar to the so-called transaction tax, but not for the sale and purchase of national bond tickets. According to the United States, it is obviously encouraging both parties to buy and sell bond tickets with all its strength. Moreover, the transaction of national bond tickets is promoted by the government to promote bond tickets, and the society promotes financial activities. Whether it is spot trading or futures trading, the benefits obtained are all approved by national policies and should not be considered speculation. In all countries in the East and the West, the long-term transaction of national bond tickets and other securities is mostly limited to two months. It is a common practice in the world for the transaction of national bond tickets to have futures. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, the Legislative Yuan stipulated the Exchange Law, which has been convenient for merchants and people for six or seven years. If the futures trading of public bonds is mistakenly considered speculation and a new tax is levied, it is

To collect is to prohibit It turns away merchants and people to other industries in search of illegitimate profits. It not only loses the essence of legislation, but is also not the blessing of the country and society. Moreover, the economic center of our country is only concentrated in the corner of the concession. In case foreigners take advantage of the market, such as the operation of bonds by a certain foreign bank, one after another. Also, if the establishment of the exchange is horizontally added, the government is distressed by the formal restraints. If a certain savings society refuses to withdraw, the rise of a storm lies in the slightest, and the cause is often created here, and the result is there. The gain is very small, and the loss is great. The country has less transaction tax, so it hinders the lively circulation of this huge amount of bond tickets, and the aspirants are gradually encroaching. Brokers dare not use dangerous words to sensationalize, nor dare to echo. Each law is drafted in the East and the West and has been deleted and is not tired of being detailed. For example, Article 7 of the Japanese Trading Tax Law is also the one revised by Law No. 6 of the Taisho year 11. The Central Political Conference, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance are the highest political organs. The new tax regulations must be consulted extensively and deliberated to perfection. If it is beneficial to the country, it will be changed in the morning and evening. There is no suspicion or taboo. Otherwise, they will go against what they like, and even if they are ordered, they will not follow. The trading tax regulations recently passed by the Legislative Yuan. The Central Political Conference, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance should be concerned about the national economy in terms of securities with prices. The transaction tax on the public bond item.

Resolutely remove It is fortunate that all the above words have been checked. The Exchange Law of our country and the trading tax to be levied are all based on foreign legislation, so the American and Japanese systems of not levying the national bond coupon transaction tax are appropriate mirrors for our country's trading tax law. Moreover, our country's public bonds have never been issued directly. They are always first mortgaged to financial institutions and must be circulated in the market through regular auctions by the exchange. Only then can the bonds be sold successively and the mortgage coupons be successively recovered. The exchange is the only medium for the circulation of national bond coupons in our country, which is different from the direct solicitation of bonds to the people in other countries. We should follow the precedent of tax exemption in the United States and Japan to help the circulation of national debt. Otherwise, teach the gibbons to climb trees, and gradually incite foreign merchants to covet and manipulate. The various malpractices listed by the Association are not over-considered. Although this tax law has been decided by the Legislative Yuan, according to the current practice, the Central Political Conference, as the highest political organ, has the power to formulate legislative principles and transfer orders for reconsideration and amendment. The hospital department is the administrative主管官署, and also has the power to raise opinions and present them to the National Government for transfer orders for reconsideration and amendment. It is reasonable to present a document based on the situation, and pray that the department will review and approve the national debt item in the transaction tax law, regardless of the spot and futures, and generally exempt taxes in accordance with the American and Japanese precedents, and handle them quickly in accordance with the legislative amendment procedures, in order to assist the circulation of bonds, which is public convenience. Respectfully presented.

Page 11

Driving from Shanghai Directly to Europe for Sightseeing

Remarks by Swedish Explorer Dr. Sven Hedin

The Possibility of Restoring the Eurasian Transportation Line of Thousands of Years Ago

Swedish explorer Dr. Sven Hedin, at the invitation of the Ministry of Railways two years ago, along with experts and technicians, went to the Northwest to survey the Sui-Xin Highway, a journey that took eighteen months. After returning to Beijing, he repeatedly met with Chairman Lin, President Wang, and others, and then went to Wuhan to meet with Chairman Chiang. He returned to Beijing a few days ago, and that evening, he and his assistant, Dr. Norin, took a train to Shanghai, arriving here at 7:15 yesterday morning. In the afternoon, he met with Chinese and foreign journalists to report on the trip. The details are recorded below:

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning: Dr. Hedin and his assistant, Dr. Norin, arrived at the North Station by train from Beijing at 7:15 yesterday morning. Those who went to the station to welcome him included the Swedish Chargé d'Affaires in China, Mr. Lin Guisi, and the Chairman of the Swedish Association, Mr. Norman, and others. After getting off the train, the doctor went directly to the Swedish Consul General's residence at No. 1 Kai Na Road to rest. He plans to meet with Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu in Shanghai and stay for three or four days before returning to Peiping and taking the Siberian Railway back to Europe.

Describing the Experience: At 2:30 yesterday afternoon, Dr. Hedin hosted reporters from Chinese and Western newspapers at his residence, vividly describing his experience for two hours. The journey was full of hardships, and his descriptions from the perspective of a geologist and archaeologist were particularly interesting. Dr. Hedin began by saying, "I came to China on August 23, 1933, at the invitation of the Chinese Ministry of Railways to survey the Huan-Xin Highway. Accompanying me were three technicians from the Ministry of Railways, Swedish physician Dr. Homan, Swedish archaeologist Professor Pan Meng, and others, as well as four automobiles. We departed from Peiping on October 25, 1933, first to Guihua, and then through the Inner Mongolian desert, arriving in Hami, Xinjiang, on February 6 of last year. The entire journey was 2,000 kilometers long, and the entire route is indeed the most suitable automobile highway."

Rich Resources of Xinjiang: The doctor continued, "The area of ​​Xinjiang Province is almost equal to the entire Europe, with an area of ​​5 million square miles, and a population of only 3.5 million people. 90% of its land is desert, the continent farthest from the coastline in the world. Its resources are extremely astonishing, with very rich gold, silver, and other mines. West of Hami, there is a huge oil field. I once explored there 45 years ago and discovered mountain ranges parallel to the Himalayas, and the ancient city of Loulan from the Han Dynasty. Thousands of years ago, Eurasian transportation passed through this vast desert, through Xinjiang, and to Xi'an. During the Tang Dynasty, Chinese silk was transported to Rome through this route."

Disturbances Obstructed: "After we arrived in Hami, we went further west to Turpan, where we encountered disturbances in Xinjiang and the outbreak of war, experiencing great difficulties. Finally, we reached Aksu, on the border of the Soviet Union, through Toksun, Korla, Kuqa. My four cars were initially detained by the rebels as tools for escape, and later borrowed by Sheng Shicai's army for pursuit. After being detained for several months, and the disturbances subsided, Governor Sheng sent a guard of 50 soldiers to escort us out of the country. The four cars were also undamaged. On the way back, we passed through Hami, Anxi, Dunhuang, Yumen, Suzhou, Ganzhou, Liangzhou, Lanzhou, and reached Xi'an in Shaanxi, and returned to Nanjing on February 14 of this year via the Longhai Railway."

Eurasian Transportation: "As a result of this survey, the plan for the Huan-Xin Highway, that is (1) from Guihua via the Inner Mongolia Road to Hami, (2) from Xi'an via Lanzhou, Liangzhou, Ganzhou, Suzhou, Yumen, Dunhuang, Anxi to Hami. Both lines have original routes to follow and are easy to achieve. From Hami through Turpan, Korla, Kuqa to Aksu, on the border between China and Russia, there is a small section. If the Soviet Russian government approves it and connects it to the Soviet Russian highway, it can directly reach Europe. The Eurasian transportation line of thousands of years ago is expected to be restored and realized in the near future. In other words, if cars can pass from Shanghai to Guihua, then you can drive directly from Shanghai to Europe for sightseeing. As for the railway construction plan, it requires huge sums of money and considerable time, which is not easy to talk about," he said.

Sven Hedin

Soviet Russian Influence: The doctor finally said, "Before I set off, I was instructed by the Ministry of Railways that, in addition to surveying the highway, I should absolutely not involve myself in political issues. Therefore, everyone in Xinjiang was a friend. As for Soviet Russia's presence there, there is no special influence, only that trade is indeed progressing day by day. After returning to Beijing this time, I was treated with great courtesy by Chairman Lin, President Wang, and others, and I am extremely grateful," he said. The doctor is already 70 years old, his hair is gray, but his spirit is exceptionally full, and he lectured for nearly two hours without fatigue. His courageous and adventurous spirit is worthy of our admiration.
